parameterization for specific field types, allowing backend-specific optimizations while maintaining safety.\\n\\n## Key Safety Principles\\n\\n1. **Separation of Concerns**: SQL and parameters are always kept as separate values throughout the execution chain\\n2. **Placeholder System**: All dynamic values use '%s' or backend-specific placeholders rather than string concatenation\\n3.
